   // om namo buddhāya //	// om namaH budDAya //
   Saundaranandaṃ Mahākāvyam	SOndara-nandam MahAkAvyam
   prathamaḥ sargaḥ	praTamaH sargaH
   kapilavastu varṇana	kapilavastu varNana
   gautamaḥ kapilo nāma munirdharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ /	gOtamaH kapilaH nAma muniH-Darma-BRtAm varaH /
   babhūva tapasi śrāntaḥ kākṣīvāniva gautamaḥ // Saund_1.1 //	baBUva tapasi SrAntaH kAkzIvAn-iva gOtamaH // SOnd-_1.1 //
   aśiśriyadyaḥ satataṃ dīptaṃ kāśyapavattapaḥ /	aSiSriyat-yaH satatam dIptam kASyapa-vat-tapaH /
   āśiśrāya ca tadvṛddhau siddhiṃ kāśyapavat parām // Saund_1.2 //	ASiSrAya ca tad-vRdDO sidDim kASyapa-vat parAm // SOnd-_1.2 //
   haviḥṣu yaśca svātmārthaṃ gāmadhukṣad vasiṣṭhavat /	haviHzu yaH-ca sva-Atma-arTam gAm-aDukzat vasizWa-vat /
   tapaḥśiṣṭeṣu ca śiṣyeṣu gāmadhukṣad vasiṣṭhavat // Saund_1.3 //	tapaH-Sizwezu ca Sizyezu gAm-aDukzat vasizWa-vat // SOnd-_1.3 //
   māhātmyāddīrghatapaso yo dvitīya ivābhavat /	mAhAtmyAt-dIrGa-tapasaH yaH dvitIyaH iva-aBavat /
   tṛtīya iva yaścābhūt kāvyāṅgirasayordhiyā // Saund_1.4 //	tRtIyaH iva yaH-ca-aBUt kAvya-AFgirasayoH-DiyA // SOnd-_1.4 //
   tasya vistīrṇatapasaḥ pārśve himavataḥ śubhe /	tasya vistIrNa-tapasaH pArSve himavataH SuBe /
   kṣetraṃ cāyatanaṃ caiva tapasāmāśramo 'bhavat // Saund_1.5 //	kzetram ca-Ayatanam ca-eva tapasAm-ASramaH aBavat // SOnd-_1.5 //
   cāruvīruttaruvanaḥ prasnigdhamṛduśādvalaḥ /	cAru-vIruttaru-vanaH prasnigDa-mRdu-SAdvalaH /
   havirdhūmavitānena yaḥ sadābhra ivābabhau // Saund_1.6 //	haviH-DUma-vitAnena yaH sadA-aBraH iva-AbaBO // SOnd-_1.6 //
   mṛdubhiḥ saikataiḥ snigdhaiḥ kesarāstarapāṇḍubhiḥ /	mRduBiH sEkatEH snigDEH kesara-Astara-pANxuBiH /
   bhūmibhāgairasaṃkīrṇaiḥ sāṅgarāga ivābhavat // Saund_1.7 //	BUmi-BAgEH-asaMkIrNEH sa-aFgarAgaH iva-aBavat // SOnd-_1.7 //

   ākīrṇo 'pi tapobhṛddhiḥ śūnyaśūnya ivābhavat // Saund_1.10 //	AkIrNaH api tapaH-BRt-DiH SUnya-SUnyaH iva-aBavat // SOnd-_1.10 //
   agnīnāṃ hūyamānānāṃ śikhināṃ kūjatāmapi /	agnInAm hUyamAnAnAm SiKinAm kUjatAm-api /
   tīrthānāṃ cābhiṣekeṣu śuśruve yatra niḥsvanaḥ // Saund_1.11 //	tIrTAnAm ca-aBizekezu SuSruve yatra niHsvanaH // SOnd-_1.11 //
   virejurhariṇā yatra suptā medhyāsu vediṣu /	virejuH-hariNA yatra suptAH meDyAsu vedizu /
   salājairmādhavīpuṣpairupahārāḥ kṛtā iva // Saund_1.12 //	sa-lAjEH-mADavI-puzpEH-upahArAH kRtAH iva // SOnd-_1.12 //

   saṃdigdhe 'pyapunarbhāve viruddheṣvāgameṣvapi /	saMdigDe api-apunarBAve virudDezu-Agamezu-api /

   yatra sma mīyate brahma kaiścit kaiścinna mīyate /	yatra sma mIyate brahma kEScid kEScid-na mIyate /
   kāle nimīyate somo na cākāle pramīyate // Saund_1.15 //	kAle nimIyate somaH na ca-akAle pramIyate // SOnd-_1.15 //
   nirapekṣāḥ śarīreṣu dharme yatra svabuddhayaḥ /	nirapekzAH SarIrezu Darme yatra sva-budDayaH /
   saṃhṛṣṭā iva yatnena tāpasāstepire tapaḥ // Saund_1.16 //	saMhRzwAH iva yatnena tApasAH-tepire tapaH // SOnd-_1.16 //
   śrāmyanto munayo yatra svargāyodyuktacetasaḥ /	SrAmyantaH munayaH yatra svargAya-udyukta-cetasaH /
   taporāgeṇa dharmasya vilopamiva cakrire // Saund_1.17 //	tapaH-rAgeNa Darmasya vilopam-iva cakrire // SOnd-_1.17 //

   pātraṃ śabdasya mahataḥ śriyāṃ ca vinayasya ca // Saund_1.19 //	pAtram Sabdasya mahataH SriyAm ca vinayasya ca // SOnd-_1.19 //
   arharūpā hyanarhasya mahātmānaścalātmanaḥ /	arha-rUpA hi-anarhasya mahAtmAnaH-cala-AtmanaH /
   prājñāḥ prajñāvimuktasya bhrātṛvyasya yavīyasaḥ // Saund_1.20 //	prAjQAH prajQA-vimuktasya BrAtRvyasya yavIyasaH // SOnd-_1.20 //
   mātṛśulkādupagatāṃ te śriyaṃ [ca] viṣehire /	mAtR-SulkAt-upagatAm te Sriyam [ca] vizehire /
   rarakṣuśca pituḥ satyaṃ yasmācchiśiyire vanam // Saund_1.21 //	rarakzuH-ca pituH satyam yasmAt-SiSiyire vanam // SOnd-_1.21 //
   teṣāṃ munirupādhyāyo gautamaḥ kapilo 'bhavat /	tezAm muniH-upADyAyaH gOtamaH kapilaH aBavat /
   gurugotrādataḥ kautsāste bhavanti sma gautamāḥ // Saund_1.22 //	guru-gotrAt-atas kOtsAH-te Bavanti sma gOtamAH // SOnd-_1.22 //
   ekapitroryathā bhrātroḥ pṛthagguruparigrahāt /	eka-pitroH-yaTA BrAtroH pRTak-guru-parigrahAt /
   rāma evābhavad gārgyo vāsubhadro 'pi gautamaḥ // Saund_1.23 //	rAmaH eva-aBavat gArgyaH vAsuBadraH api gOtamaH // SOnd-_1.23 //
   śākavṛkṣapraticchannaṃ vāsaṃ yasmācca cakrire /	SAka-vRkza-praticCannam vAsam yasmAt-ca cakrire /
   tasmādikṣvākuvaṃśyāste bhuvi śākyā iti smṛtāḥ // Saund_1.24 //	tasmAt-ikzvAku-vaMSyAH-te Buvi SAkyAH iti smRtAH // SOnd-_1.24 //
   sa teṣāṃ gautamaścakre svavaṃśasadṛśīḥ kriyāḥ /	sa tezAm gOtamaH-cakre sva-vaMSa-sadRSIH kriyAH /
   munirūrdhvaṃ kumārasya sagarasyeva bhārgavaḥ // Saund_1.25 //	muniH-UrDvam kumArasya sagarasya-iva BArgavaH // SOnd-_1.25 //
   kaṇvaḥ śākuntalasyeva bharatasya tarasvinaḥ /	kaNvaH SAkuntalasya-iva Baratasya tarasvinaH /
   vālmikiriva dhīmāṃśca dhīmatormaithileyayoḥ // Saund_1.26 //	vAlmikiH-iva DImAn=-ca DImatoH-mETileyayoH // SOnd-_1.26 //
   tadvanaṃ muninā tena taiśca kṣatriyapuṅgavaiḥ /	tat-vanam muninA tena tEH-ca kzatriya-puFgavEH /
   śāntāṃ guptāṃ ca yugapad brahmakṣatraśriyaṃ dadhe // Saund_1.27 //	SAntAm guptAm ca yugapad brahma-kzatra-Sriyam daDe // SOnd-_1.27 //
   athodakalaśaṃ gṛhya teṣāṃ vṛddhicikīrṣayā /	aTa-udakalaSam gRhya tezAm vRdDi-cikIrzayA /
   muniḥ sa viyadutpatya tānuvāca nṛpātmajān // Saund_1.28 //	muniH sa viyat-utpatya tAn-uvAca nRpa-AtmajAn // SOnd-_1.28 //
   yā patet kalaśādasmādakṣayyasalilānmahīm /	yA patet kalaSAt-asmAt-akzayya-salilAt-mahIm /
   dhārā tāmanatikramya māmanveta yathākramam // Saund_1.29 //	DArA tAm-anatikramya mAm-anveta yaTAkramam // SOnd-_1.29 //

   rathānāruruhuḥ sarve śīghravāhānalaṃkṛtān // Saund_1.30 //	raTAn-AruruhuH sarve SIGra-vAhAn-alaMkRtAn // SOnd-_1.30 //
   tataḥ sa tairanugataḥ syandanasthairnabhogataḥ /	tatas sa tEH-anugataH syandana-sTEH-naBaH-gataH /
   tadāśramamahīprāntaṃ paricikṣepa vāriṇā // Saund_1.31 //	tad-ASrama-mahI-prAntam paricikzepa vAriNA // SOnd-_1.31 //
   aṣṭāpadamivālikhya nimittaiḥ surabhīkṛtam /	azwApadam-iva-AliKya nimittEH suraBIkRtam /

   asmin dhārāparikṣipte nemicinhitalakṣaṇe /	asmin DArA-parikzipte nemi-cinhita-lakzaNe /
   nirmimīdhvaṃ puraṃ yūyaṃ mayi yāte triviṣṭapam // Saund_1.33 //	nirmimIDvam puram yUyam mayi yAte trivizwapam // SOnd-_1.33 //
   tataḥ kadācitte vīrāstasmin pratigate munau /	tatas kadAcid-te vIrAH-tasmin pratigate munO /
   babhramuyauṃvanoddāmā gajā iva niraṅkuśā // Saund_1.34 //	baBramuyOMvana-uddAmAH gajAH iva niraFkuSAH // SOnd-_1.34 //

   vedavedāṅgaviduṣastasthuṣaḥ ṣaṭsu karmasu /	veda-vedAFga-viduzaH-tasTuzaH zawsu karmasu /

   yasmādanyāyataste ca kaṃcinnācīkaran karam /	yasmAt-anyAyataH-te ca kaMcid-na-acIkaran karam /

   kakandasya makandasya kuśāmbasyeva cāśrame /	kakandasya makandasya kuSAmbasya-iva ca-ASrame /

   āpuḥ puraṃ tatpuruhūtakalpāste tejasāryeṇa na vismayena /	ApuH puram tad-puruhUta-kalpAH-te tejasA-AryeNa na vismayena /
   āpuryaśogandhamataśca śaśvat sutā yayāteriva kīrtimantaḥ // Saund_1.59 //	ApuH-yaSaH-ganDam-atas-ca SaSvat sutA yayAteH-iva kIrtimantaH // SOnd-_1.59 //
   tannāthavṛttairapi rājaputrairarājakaṃ naiva rarāja rāṣṭram /	tat-nATa-vRttEH-api rAja-putrEH-arAjakam na-eva rarAja rAzwram /
   tārāsahastrairapi dīpyamānairanutthite candra ivāntarīkṣam // Saund_1.60	tArAsa-hastrEH-api dIpyamAnEH-anutTite candraH iva-antarIkzam // SOnd_1.60
   yo jyāyānatha vayasā guṇaiśca teṣāṃ bhātṝṇāṃ vṛṣabha ivaujasā vṛṣāṇām /	yaH jyAyAn-aTa vayasA guNEH-ca tezAm BAtLNAm vRzaBaH iva-ojasA vRzANAm /
   te tatra priyaguravastamabhyaṣicannādityā daśaśatalocanaṃ divīva //	te tatra priya-guravaH-tam-aByazicanna-AdityAH daSa-Sata-locanam divi-iva //
   Saund_1.61 //	SOnd-_1.61 //
   ācāravānvinayavānnayavānkriyāvān dharmāya nendriyasukhāya dhṛtātapatraḥ /	AcAravAn-vinayavAn-nayavAn-kriyAvAn DarmAya na-indriya-suKAya DRta-AtapatraH /
   tadbhrātṛbhiḥ parivṛtaḥ sa jugopa rāṣṭram saṃkrandano divamivānusṛto	tad-BrAtRBiH parivRtaH sa jugopa rAzwram saMkrandanaH divam-iva-anusRtaH-
